<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knaagdier.html>knaagdier</a> (22810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knagen.html>knagen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to gnaw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">animal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, perhaps through  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Nagetier</i>, eventually after  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rodens</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knaap.html>knaap</a> (5232)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnāpe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">cnapo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knappô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">boy, youth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gnebʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to press, tighten</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:knappe.html>Knappe</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knabe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">knave</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">knape</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">knabe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">knapi</i>.
</p>

<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">knabbern</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to nibble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Both could ultimately be from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gnet-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to press</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>, or imitative.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>

***knakworst.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knakworst.html>knakworst</a> (69249)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Mentioned by Kiliaen. From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knakken.html>knakken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to crack</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:worst.html>worst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sausage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knackwurst</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knalpot.html>knalpot</a> (64396)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knal.html>knal</a></i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knallen.html>knallen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a>, to make a loud, sharp noise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knalpot.html>knalpot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knalpotten.html>knalpotten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knalpot.html>knalpotje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>muffler, silencer <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of an exhaust pipe</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<p>Unknown. Found only in Dutch and Low German (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:knapp.html>knapp</a></i>).

***knapp.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knapp.html>knapp</a> (39335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:knap.html>knap</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knap.html>knap</a></i>, whose sense “pretty” also occurs in old German attestations and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> thought to be derived from “tight” <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> “tightly fitting” (of a piece of clothing). Further origin unsettled.  Also compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">næppe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hardly at all</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:knapp.html>knapp</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de comparative-form-of" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:knapper.html>knapper</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-de superlative-form-of" lang="de">am knappsten</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>scarce</li>
<li>lean <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">having little <a href = vnd.unilang:extra.html>extra</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>somewhat less (than)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">ein <b>knappes</b> Jahr</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">a little less than a year</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> short or tight</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:knapp.html>knapp</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>narrowly; just
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Wir <a href = vnd.unilang:sind.html>sind</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:knapp.html>knapp</a></b> pünktlich.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>’re <b>just</b> in time.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>somewhat less than, almost
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:sein.html>Sein</a> Sohn ist <b><a href = vnd.unilang:knapp.html>knapp</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:acht.html>acht</a> Jahre alt.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">His son <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> just under eight years old/<a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> almost eight years old.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de">Es ist <b><a href = vnd.unilang:knapp.html>knapp</a></b> sieben Uhr.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It's just before seven <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>'clock/almost seven <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>'clock.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="de">gut</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knappen.html>knappen</a></i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knap.html>knap</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zak.html>zak</a></i>. 16th century.

</p>

***knarsen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knarsen.html>knarsen</a> (33279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knarsen.html>knarsen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to creak; to make a high-pitched, grating noise</li>
<li>to grind (one's teeth together)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>Met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tanden.html>tanden</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:knarsen.html>knarsen</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slaap.html>slaap</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geeft.html>geeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geluid.html>geluid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slecht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebit.html>gebit</a>.</i>: Grinding your teeth in your sleep <a href = vnd.unilang:lets.html>lets</a> out an unpleasant noise and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> bad for your denture.</dd></dl></li></ol>

***knecht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knecht.html>knecht</a> (11868)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnecht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kneht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knehtaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:knecht.html>Knecht</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">knight</i>.
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kneden.html>kneden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to knead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bom.html>bom</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bomb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnuut</i>, <span class="Latn" lang="dum">cnuyt</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jackdaw, crow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnoteren</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnueteren</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cneuteren</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to twitter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***kneus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kneus.html>kneus</a> (23789)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kneuzen.html>kneuzen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hurt, bruise, grind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kneus.html>kneus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kneuzen.html>kneuzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kneusje.html>kneusje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A bruise, hurt body part (notably skin) without an open wound</li>
<li>A bruised egg</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A violation, infraction</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An inferior worker, unproductive winer</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any weakling, <a href = vnd.unilang:softie.html>softie</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***knie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knie.html>knie</a> (4655)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*cnio</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knewą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵónu</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knie.html>knie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knie.html>knieën</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knietje.html>knietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A knee.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A kneeing, a prod or blow with the knee.</li></ol>

***knielen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knielen.html>knielen</a> (8397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:knielen.html>knielen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kniolon</i>. Ultimately derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knie.html>knie</a></i>, but the source of the <i>l</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unknown.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knielen.html>knielen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to kneel (stoop down and <a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a> on the knee)</li></ol>

***knijpen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knijpen.html>knijpen</a> (6846)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">knipen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*knīpen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knīpaną</i>. Likely related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nijpen.html>nijpen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knijpen.html>knijpen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to pinch, squeeze</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***knikken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knikken.html>knikken</a> (15802)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnicken</i>; related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neigen.html>neigen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bend, turn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">nicken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to nod</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:neigen.html>neigen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikken.html>knikken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to nod as in to express agreement.</li></ol>

***knikker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knikker.html>knikker</a> (19182)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikken.html>knikken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knikkoną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fold, <a href = vnd.unilang:snap.html>snap</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> imitative.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikker.html>knikker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikkers.html>knikkers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikker.html>knikkertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a marble <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">toy</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>various similarly shaped <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a>, including:
<ol><li>a billiards ball</li>
<li>certain seeds</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a head, especially a bald skull (typically in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kale.html>kale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:knikker.html>knikker</a></i>)</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a lump or stone</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(in the plural, absolutely used with definite article: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:knikkers.html>knikkers</a></b>)</i> The stakes of a game, deal etc.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">marbel</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuiter.html>stuiter</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span>: the root of <a href = vnd.unilang:knikken.html>knikken</a> 'to nod' + <a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikker.html>knikker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikkers.html>knikkers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikker.html>knikkertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A nodder</li></ol>

***knippen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knippen.html>knippen</a> (5101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:knippen.html>knippen</a></i>, further etymology unknown. Directly related only with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:knippen.html>knippen</a></i>. Probably onomatopoeic.
</p><p>The sense “to blink” may, at least in part, be due to conflation with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knijpen.html>knijpen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to squeeze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ogen.html>ogen</a></i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">toeknijpen</i> (“to screw up one’s eyes”); also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:knippen.html>knippen</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">kniepen</i> both in the sense of “to blink”, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kniepen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knippen.html>knippen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cut with scissors</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cut (remove an item and place it in memory for <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> use)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make a pinching movement, especially with one's eyelids; thus, to blink</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:snap.html>snap</a> one's <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a></li></ol>

</p>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">knobbe</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knappô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">button</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  Compare regional German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knubbel</i> as well as <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knopf</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">button</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***knoeien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knoeien.html>knoeien</a> (13731)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knoeien.html>knoeien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to create a mess</li>
<li>to mess around</li>
<li>to defraud</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">kliederen</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prutsen.html>prutsen</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">knofloick</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">knuuflooch</i>, a dissimilated variant of earlier <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cloffloc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clove-leek</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klieven.html>klieven</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">look</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knoblauch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">knyflok</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">clove</i>.

***knokkel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knokkel.html>knokkel</a> (74914)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnokel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*knukil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knukilaz</i>, a diminutive of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knukô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (whence <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">knook</i>). Thus, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> synchronically equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">knook</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-el</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">diminutive <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">knuckle</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knöchel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knochen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">kno</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">knoge</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knokkel.html>knokkel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knokkel.html>knokkels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knokkel.html>knokkeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>finger-joint; knuckle</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">vingergewricht</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***knoll.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a> (74911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">cnoll</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">summit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knudan-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knudla-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knulla-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">cnotta</i>.
</p><p>Related to Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">knollr</i> (found only in names of <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a>), Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knol.html>knol</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tuber</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Swedish <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">knöl</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tuber</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Danish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">knold</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hillock, clod, tuber</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knolle</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bulb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">knolls</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A small mound or rounded hill.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1813</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walter_Scott" class="extiw" title="w:Walter Scott"><a href = vnd.unilang:walter.html>Walter</a> Scott</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rokeby" class="extiw" title="w:Rokeby">Rokeby</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">On <b><a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a></b> or hillock rears his crest, / Lonely and huge, the giant oak.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b> January–February,  <a href = vnd.unilang:matt.html>Matt</a> Bean,  “Your cultural calendar: 7 <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> to look forward to this year”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Men%27s_Health" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Men | s Health"><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>Men</a>'s Health</a></cite>, volume 23, number 1, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Standard_Serial_Number" class="extiw" title="w:International Standard Serial Number">ISSN</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.worldcat.org/issn/1054-4836">1054-4836</a></small>, page <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=6ccDAAAAMBAJamp;pg=PA135amp;dq=%22knoll%22">135</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In the northern hemisphere, June 21 <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> the most daylight <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a>. Pack a picnic—a chilled bottle of Sancerre, cheese, olives, and a nice baguette—and hit the grassy <b><a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Imitative, or variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">knell</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">knolls</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A knell.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">knolls</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">knolling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">knolled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href = vnd.unilang:ring.html>ring</a> (a bell) mournfully; to knell.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To sound, like a bell; to knell.
<ul><li><i>c</i>. <b>1599</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/As_You_Like_It" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:As You Like It">As You Like It</a></i>, Act II, scene VII, 114
<dl><dd>If ever <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> where bells have <b>knoll´d</b> to church.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1815</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lord_Byron" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lord Byron">Lord Byron</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Works_of_Lord_Byron_(ed._Coleridge,_Prothero)/Poetry/Volume_3/Parisina" class="extiw" title="s:The Works of Lord Byron (ed. Coleridge, Prothero)/Poetry/Volume 3/Parisina">Parisina</a></i>
<dl><dd>For a departed being's soul / The death hymn peals, and the hollow bells <b><a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>?</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alfred_Tennyson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alfred Tennyson">Alfred Tennyson</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Gardener%27s_Daughter;_or,_the_Pictures" class="extiw" title="s:The Gardener | s Daughter; or, the Pictures">The Gardener's Daughter; or, The Pictures</a></i>
<dl><dd>Heavy clocks <b>knolling</b> the drowsy <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Named after <a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>Knoll</a>, a furniture fabrication shop, famous for its angular range of designer furniture.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">knolls</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">knolling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">knolled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To arrange related <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> in parallel or at 90 degree angles.</li></ol>
</body>
